The body and attributes are structured OTel key-value pairs. The formatter uses substitution expressions to populate fields, but the wire format is structured OTLP, not raw text or JSON.\\n\\n**5. The record is a protobuf Struct with access log command operators as values. This is structured, NOT plain text.\\n\\n**6. Summary\\n\\n- **Structured (JSON) logging**: `file` and `stream` (stdout/stderr) sinks support JSON output via `SubstitutionFormatString` with `json_format`.
